class="post-66 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-economia ast-grid-common-col ast-full-width ast-article-post remove-featured-img-padding" id="post-66" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork" itemscope="itemscope"><div class="ast-post-format- blog-layout-4 ast-article-inner"><div class="post-content ast-grid-common-col" ><div class="ast-blog-featured-section post-thumb ast-blog-single-element"><div class="post-thumb-img-content post-thumb"><a href="https://www.momentofinanceiro.com.br/dicas-para-economizar-no-supermercado/" aria-label="Read: Dicas para economizar no supermercado" ><img fetchpriority="high" width="600" height="400" src="https://www.momentofinanceiro.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/supermercado-como-economizar-momento-financeiro.png" class="attachment-large size-large wp-post-image" alt="" itemprop="image" decoding="async" srcset="https://www.momentofinanceiro.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/supermercado-como-economizar-momento-financeiro.png 600w, https://www.momentofinanceiro.com.br/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/supermercado-como-economizar-momento-financeiro-300x200.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px" /></a></div></div><h2 class="entry-title ast-blog-single-element" itemprop="headline"><a href="https://www.momentofinanceiro.com.br/dicas-para-economizar-no-supermercado/" rel="bookmark">Dicas para economizar no supermercado</a></h2><div class="ast-excerpt-container ast-blog-single-element"><p>Um dos hábitos que muitos brasileiros têm, é ir frenquentemente no mercado.
